I've been giving Portra 160 a go at night and I often get very contrasty negs with hightlights blown away, yet very little detail in dark areas. I don't use a meter at night but studied the Ultimate Exposure Computer for help on what the right exposures should be. One issue you might be having is in the scanning of your film. Shots I take in the daytime are no problem, but my night shots are much more difficult to get right and I'm often scanning the same frame, under different settings, several times before I'm satisfied.\n\nWhen it comes to getting contrasty negatives, that happens to me sometimes too.
